```python
import numpy as np
import pandas as pd
np.random.seed(12345)#设置伪随机数生成器的种子起点，保证实验结果一致
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
plt.rc('figure',figsize=(10,6))#格式设置
np.set_printoptions(precision=4,suppress=True)#格式设置
```


```python
!type Desktop\pydata-book\examples\ex1.csv
```

    a,b,c,d,message
    1,2,3,4,hello
    5,6,7,8,world
    9,10,11,12,foo
    


```python
df=pd.read_csv('Desktop/pydata-book/examples/ex1.csv')
df
```

```python
#read_table 允许自己指定分隔符
#这里用sep指定‘，’为默认分隔符
pd.read_table('Desktop/pydata-book/examples/ex1.csv',sep=',')
```

```python
#header参数  有的文件没有头行，比如下面这个
!type Desktop\pydata-book\examples\ex2.csv
```

    1,2,3,4,hello
    5,6,7,8,world
    9,10,11,12,foo
    


```python
#设置header=None,会默认给个数字当表头
pd.read_csv('Desktop\pydata-book\examples\ex2.csv',header=None)
```

```python
#参数names
#或者，用names=自己设置表头
pd.read_csv('Desktop\pydata-book\examples\ex2.csv',names=['a','b','c','d','message'])
```

```python
#参数index_col
#如果你想指定第四列为索引，可以使用，index_col=
names=['a','b','c','d','message']
pd.read_csv('Desktop\pydata-book\examples\ex2.csv',names=names,index_col='message')
```

```python
#想要设置分层所以
#如打类分成两个one two
#one 下面分4个abcd
#two 下面分4个abcd
#我们看下面这个文件
!type Desktop\pydata-book\examples\csv_mindex.csv
```

    key1,key2,value1,value2
    one,a,1,2
    one,b,3,4
    one,c,5,6
    one,d,7,8
    two,a,9,10
    two,b,11,12
    two,c,13,14
    two,d,15,16
    


```python
#则使用index_col指定两列索引['key1','key2']
parsed=pd.read_csv('Desktop\pydata-book\examples\csv_mindex.csv',index_col=['key1','key2'])
parsed
```

```python
#使用正则表达式做分隔符
#有的时候，一张表的分隔符不是固定的，考虑下面这种情况
list(open('Desktop\pydata-book\examples\ex3.txt'))
```




    ['            A         B         C\n',
     'aaa -0.264438 -1.026059 -0.619500\n',
     'bbb  0.927272  0.302904 -0.032399\n',
     'ccc -0.264273 -0.386314 -0.217601\n',
     'ddd -0.871858 -0.348382  1.100491\n']




```python
#该文档是数量不确定的空格分隔，指定分隔符为正则表达式\s+
result = pd.read_table('Desktop\pydata-book\examples\ex3.txt',sep='\s+')
result
```

```python
#本例中，由于列名的数量少一个，read_table会自动推断第一列为索引
#skiprows
#解析异常，如下面这个文档
!type Desktop\pydata-book\examples\ex4.csv
```

    # hey!
    a,b,c,d,message
    # just wanted to make things more difficult for you
    # who reads CSV files with computers, anyway?
    1,2,3,4,hello
    5,6,7,8,world
    9,10,11,12,foo
    


```python
#这里面有一行注释行
#使用skiprows=[0,2,3]跳过
pd.read_csv('Desktop\pydata-book\examples\ex4.csv',skiprows=[0,2,3])
```

```python
#处理缺失值
#通常pandas中用NULL或NA来标记
!type Desktop\pydata-book\examples\ex5.csv
```

    something,a,b,c,d,message
    one,1,2,3,4,NA
    two,5,6,,8,world
    three,9,10,11,12,foo
    


```python
pd.read_csv('Desktop\pydata-book\examples\ex5.csv')
```

```python
#na_values
#可以传入一个类表或者一组字符串来指定缺失值
result=pd.read_csv('Desktop\pydata-book\examples\ex5.csv',na_values=['Null'])
result
```

```python
#每列可以指定不同的缺失值表示
sentinels={'message':['foo','NA'],'something':['two']}
pd.read_csv('Desktop\pydata-book\examples\ex5.csv',na_values=sentinels)
```

```python
#统计，key这列，每个元素出现的频率
chunker=pd.read_csv('Desktop\pydata-book\examples\ex6.csv',chunksize=1000)

tot=pd.Series([])
for piece in chunker:
    tot = tot.add(piece['key'].value_counts(),fill_value=0)
    
tot=tot.sort_values(ascending=False)
tot[:10]
```

    <ipython-input-38-89ac42b3b485>:4: DeprecationWarning: The default dtype for empty Series will be 'object' instead of 'float64' in a future version. Specify a dtype explicitly to silence this warning.

```python
##6.1.2 将数据写入文本格式
import numpy as np
import pandas as pd
np.random.seed(12345)#设置伪随机数生成器的种子起点，保证实验结果一致
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
plt.rc('figure',figsize=(10,6))
np.set_printoptions(precision=4,suppress=True)
```

```python
#读出文本，读出的变量存在data里
data=pd.read_csv('Desktop\pydata-book\examples\ex5.csv')
data
```

```python
#sys.stdout输出到屏幕，但是，使用|分割
import sys
data.to_csv(sys.stdout,sep='|')
```

    |something|a|b|c|d|message
    0|one|1|2|3.0|4|
    1|two|5|6||8|world
    2|three|9|10|11.0|12|foo



```python
#缺失值使用NULL填充缺失值
data.to_csv(sys.stdout,na_rep='NULL')
```

    ,something,a,b,c,d,message
    0,one,1,2,3.0,4,NULL
    1,two,5,6,NULL,8,world
    2,three,9,10,11.0,12,foo



```python
#写入文档，去掉index,去掉header
data.to_csv(sys.stdout,index=False,header=False)
```

    one,1,2,3.0,4,
    two,5,6,,8,world
    three,9,10,11.0,12,foo

```python
#写入文档，列名为abc
data.to_csv(sys.stdout,index=False,columns=['a','b','c'])
```

```python
#生成时间数据，从2000年1月1日开始，期限为7天
dates=pd.date_range('1/1/2000',periods=7)
#可以看到这里的数据类型是datetime
dates
```




    DatetimeIndex(['2000-01-01', '2000-01-02', '2000-01-03', '2000-01-04',
                   '2000-01-05', '2000-01-06', '2000-01-07'],
                  dtype='datetime64[ns]', freq='D')




```python
#生成0-6七个数字，索引为刚才生成的日期
ts=pd.Series(np.arange(7),index=dates)
ts
```

    2000-01-02    1
    2000-01-03    2
    2000-01-04    3

```python
###6.1.3 处理分割格式
#有些情况read_csv解决不了
!type Desktop\pydata-book\examples\ex7.csv
```

    "a","b","c"
    "1","2","3"
    "1","2","3"
    


```python
#对于这种带双引号的文档，首先导入csv包，读出csv文件
import csv
f=open('Desktop\pydata-book\examples\ex7.csv')
reader=csv.reader(f)
```


```python
#读出来的reader是一个可迭代对象
reader
```




    <_csv.reader at 0x20439a934c0>




```python
#需要用for循环读出来
for line in reader:
    print(line)
    print(type(line))
```

    ['a', 'b', 'c']
    <class 'list'>
    ['1', '2', '3']
    <class 'list'>
    ['1', '2', '3']
    <class 'list'>
    


```python
#可以看到是类似列表的东西
#将文件读取为行的列表
with open('Desktop\pydata-book\examples\ex7.csv') as f:
    lines=list(csv.reader(f))
lines
```




    [['a', 'b', 'c'], ['1', '2', '3'], ['1', '2', '3']]




```python
#哦~所以这个可迭代对象，就是缺个马甲
with open('Desktop\pydata-book\examples\ex7.csv') as f:
    lines=tuple(csv.reader(f))
lines
```




    (['a', 'b', 'c'], ['1', '2', '3'], ['1', '2', '3'])




```python
with open('Desktop\pydata-book\examples\ex7.csv') as f:
    lines=list(csv.reader(f))
header,values=lines[0],lines[1:]
header
```




    ['a', 'b', 'c']




```python
values
```




    [['1', '2', '3'], ['1', '2', '3']]




```python
#再拆成字典格式
data_dict={h:v for h,v in zip(header,zip(*values))}
data_dict
```




    {'a': ('1', '1'), 'b': ('2', '2'), 'c': ('3', '3')}




```python
#别问，问就是背下来
```


```python
#####6.1.4 JSON Data
#一回生二回熟，JavaScript Object Notation
#常用的标准格式，比csv更自由
#看下面这个例子
obj="""
{"name":"Wes",
"places_lived":["United States","Spain","Germany"],
"pet":null,
"siblings":[{"name":"Scott","age":30,"pets":["Zeus","Zuko"]},
            {"name":"Katie","age":38,"pets":["Sixes","Stache","Cisco"]}]
}
"""
```


```python
#我们使用Python中内置的json标准库读取json文件
#json字符串转换为python形式
import json
import pandas as pd
result=json.loads(obj)
result
```




    {'name': 'Wes',
     'places_lived': ['United States', 'Spain', 'Germany'],
     'pet': None,
     'siblings': [{'name': 'Scott', 'age': 30, 'pets': ['Zeus', 'Zuko']},
      {'name': 'Katie', 'age': 38, 'pets': ['Sixes', 'Stache', 'Cisco']}]}




```python
#python形式，转换回json
asjson=json.dumps(result)
asjson
```




    '{"name": "Wes", "places_lived": ["United States", "Spain", "Germany"], "pet": null, "siblings": [{"name": "Scott", "age": 30, "pets": ["Zeus", "Zuko"]}, {"name": "Katie", "age": 38, "pets": ["Sixes", "Stache", "Cisco"]}]}'




```python
#可以自由转换数据结构
#如result变量里面的'siblings'对应的字典
#字典里面取出name和age作为列
siblings=pd.DataFrame(result['siblings'],columns=['name','age'])
siblings
```




<div>
<style scoped>
    .dataframe tbody tr th:only-of-type {
        vertical-align: middle;
    }

    .dataframe tbody tr th {
        vertical-align: top;
    }

    .dataframe thead th {
        text-align: right;
    }
</style>

  <thead>
    <tr style="text-align: right;">
      <th></th>
      <th>name</th>
      <th>age</th>
    </tr>
  </thead>

      <th>0</th>
      <td>Scott</td>
      <td>30</td>
    </tr>

```python
#下面的这个json文件
!type Desktop\pydata-book\examples\example.json
```

    [{"a": 1, "b": 2, "c": 3},
     {"a": 4, "b": 5, "c": 6},
     {"a": 7, "b": 8, "c": 9}]
    


```python
#pd.read_json可以直接把json数据集按照指定的次序转换为Series或者DataFrame
data=pd.read_json('Desktop\pydata-book\examples\example.json')
data
```




<div>
<style scoped>
    .dataframe tbody tr th:only-of-type {

        text-align: right;
    }
</style>

    </tr>
  </thead>
  <tbody>
    <tr>
      <th>0</th>
      <td>1</td>
      <td>2</td>
      <td>3</td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <th>1</th>
      <td>4</td>
      <td>5</td>
      <td>6</td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <th>2</th>
      <td>7</td>
      <td>8</td>
      <td>9</td>
    </tr>
  </tbody>
</table>
</div>




```python
#再转换为json
print(data.to_json())
```

    {"a":{"0":1,"1":4,"2":7},"b":{"0":2,"1":5,"2":8},"c":{"0":3,"1":6,"2":9}}
    


```python
#不同的保存方式
print(data.to_json(orient='records'))
```

    [{"a":1,"b":2,"c":3},{"a":4,"b":5,"c":6},{"a":7,"b":8,"c":9}]

    function findValue(li) {
    	if( li == null ) return alert("No match!");
    
    	// if coming from an AJAX call, let's use the Id as the value
    	if( !!li.extra ) var sValue = li.extra[0];
    
    	// otherwise, let's just display the value in the text box
    	else var sValue = li.selectValue;
    
    	$('#googlesearch').submit();
    	
    }
    function findValue2(li) {
    	if( li == null ) return alert("No match!");

    	// otherwise, let's just display the value in the text box
    	else var sValue = li.selectValue;

    }

    	findValue(li);
    }
    function selectItem2(li) {
    	findValue2(li);
    }
    
    $().ready(function() {
    
    	function log(event, data, formatted) {
    		$("<li>").html( !data ? "No match!" : "Selected: " + formatted).appendTo("#result");
    	}
    	
    	function formatItem(row) {
    		return row[0] + " (<strong>id: " + row[1] + "</strong>)";
    	}
    	function formatResult(row) {
    		return row[0].replace(/(<.+?>)/gi, '');

    <a href="https://www.fdic.gov/bank/individual/failed/" onclick="s_objectID=&quot;https://www.fdic.gov/bank/individual/failed/_3&quot;;return this.s_oc?this.s_oc(e):true">Failed Banks</a> &gt; 
    Failed Bank List

    <div id="content" class="failed_bank_list">
    
    	<h1 class="page_title">Failed Bank List</h1>
    
    	<p>The FDIC is often appointed as receiver for failed banks. This page contains useful information for the customers and vendors of these banks. This includes information on the acquiring bank (if applicable), how your accounts and loans are affected, and how vendors can file claims against the receivership. <a href="https://www5.fdic.gov/drrip/cs/index.asp" onclick="s_objectID=&quot;https://www5.fdic.gov/drrip/cs/index.asp_1&quot;;return this.s_oc?this.s_oc(e):true">Failed Financial Institution Contact Search</a> displays point of contact information related to failed banks.</p>
    	
    	<p>This list includes banks which have failed since October 1,2000. To search for banks that failed prior to those on this page, visit this link: <a href="https://www5.fdic.gov/hsob/SelectRpt.asp?EntryTyp=30&amp;Header=1" onclick="s_objectID=&quot;https://www5.fdic.gov/hsob/SelectRpt.asp?EntryTyp=30&amp;Header=1_1&quot;;return this.s_oc?this.s_oc(e):true">Failures and Assistance Transactions</a></p>
    
    	
    	
      
    
    <div class="table_wrapper">	
    <p class="small_screen_warning">Due to the small screen size some information is no longer visible.<br>Full information available when viewed on a larger screen.</p>
    <p><em>Click arrows next to headers to sort in Ascending or Descending order.</em> <a class="data" href="https://www.fdic.gov/bank/individual/failed/banklist.csv" onclick="s_objectID=&quot;https://www.fdic.gov/bank/individual/failed/banklist.csv_1&quot;;return this.s_oc?this.s_oc(e):true">Download Data</a></p>

```python
#pd.read_html有很多选项，但默认的情况下，会搜索并尝试解析所有包含在标签中的表格型数据，返回的结果是DataFrame对象的列表
tables = pd.read_html('Desktop/pydata-book/examples/fdic_failed_bank_list.html')
len(tables)
failures=tables[0]
failures.head()

```

```python
#####6.1.5.1 解析XML使用lxml.objectify
#XML,是一种常用的结构化数据格式，使用元数据支持分层、嵌套数据
#下面是纽约大都会交通局发布的一份关于公交、火车服务的数据集
```


```python
#使用lxml.objectify
from lxml import objectify

path='Desktop/pydata-book/datasets/mta_perf/Performance_MNR.xml'
parsed=objectify.parse(open(path))
root=parsed.getroot() #获得对XML文件的根节点的引用
root
```




    <Element PERFORMANCE at 0x2043ac80fc0>




```python
data=[]
# 存储所有数据的列表

skip_fields=['PARENT_SEQ','INDICATOR_SEQ','DESIRED_CHANGE','DECIMAL_PLACES']
#这几个标签下的值不要

for elt in root.INDICATOR:
    #一组数据
    el_data={}
    #存储该组数据的字典
    for child in elt.getchildren():
        #取出一列数据
        if child.tag in skip_fields:
            #如果这列的标签，在我们上面定义的列表里
            continue
            #舍弃，继续
        el_data[child.tag]=child.pyval
        #如果不在，标签作为key值，这列的pyval作为value值加入字典
    data.append(el_data)
    #改组数据加入总体数据列表
```


```python
len(data)
```




    648




```python
data[1]
```

Allow pandas autoconvert it to float which could be nan (default behaviour)\r\n2. Use Int64 type, which is actually quite slow to use it in large datasets spending ages in _PyEval_EvalFrameDefault\r\n\r\n#### Describe the solution you\'d like\r\n\r\nThe obvious option is to use fill value, like -1 for NaN, it currently could be done after 1st or 2nd step, with fillna and conversion to integer type back. It will be quite simple to introduce new parameter inmerge fillna={ "column1":-1,  "column2":-1} which do the same task without addition computations.\r\n\r\n#### API breaking implications\r\n\r\nBy default fillna should be None, which will keep current behaviour.\r\n\r\np.s. the same thing is reasonable for pd.concat\r\n',

bug exists on the master branch of pandas.\r\n\r\n---\r\n**Note** This issue is very similar to [Issue #8902](https://github.com/pandas-dev/pandas/issues/8902), which is fixed in `pandas==1.3.0`, but in cases where the DataFrame to concat has different columns settings as stated below, `pd.concat` is still acting weird?\r\n\r\n\r\n#### \r\n```python\r\nimport pandas as pd\r\n\r\n# pd.concat with empty DataFrame won\'t coerce type now \r\ndf = pd.DataFrame([{"col1": 1}, {"col1":2}])\r\ndf2 = pd.DataFrame({})\r\ndf_new = pd.concat([df,df2])\r\ndf_new.col1.dtype # dtype(\'int64\')\r\n\r\n# however, pd.concat with empty DataFrame with column different than the original one will still coerce type\r\ndf = pd.DataFrame([{"col1": 1}, {"col1":2}])\r\ndf2 = pd.DataFrame({}, columns=["whatever"])\r\ndf_new = pd.concat([df,df2])\r\ndf_new.col1.dtype # dtype(\'float64\')\r\n\r\n# pd.concat with empty DataFrame with same columns will still coerce type to `object`\r\ndf = pd.DataFrame([{"col1": 1}, {"col1":2}])\r\ndf2 = pd.DataFrame({}, columns=["col1"])\r\ndf_new = pd.concat([df,df2])\r\ndf_new.col1.dtype # dtype(\'object\')\r\n```\r\n\r\n#### Problem description\r\n\r\n`pd.concat` is acting inconsistently when concatenating empty DataFrame: \r\nIf the empty DataFrame is present with same column, that column is changed to `dtype(\'O\')`;\r\nIf the empty DataFrame is present with columns different than target, the target DataFrame has its original column values of type `int64` coerced to `float64`;\r\nIf the empty DataFrame is present without any column, the target DataFrame keeps its dtype;\r\n\r\n#### Expected Output\r\n\r\nI suggest just not coerce values when `pd.concat` an empty DataFrame...\r\n\r\n#### Output of And there are tools, like pytest,\r\nthat can run the examples, and make sure everything is correct.\r\n\r\nFor historical reasons, we have many examples where the code fails to run, or the\r\nactual output is different from the expected output. For example, check the next\r\nincorrect examples:\r\n\r\n```python\r\ndef add(num1, num2):\r\n    """\r\n    Computes the sum of the two numbers.\r\n\r\n    Examples\r\n    --------\r\n    >>> add(2, 2)\r\n    5\r\n\r\n    >>> add(2, 2\r\n    4\r\n\r\n    >>> add(2, number)\r\n    4\r\n\r\n    ...\r\n    """\r\n    return num1 + num2\r\n```\r\n\r\nAll them will fail for different reasons. To test the docstring of an object,\r\nthe next command can be run:\r\n\r\n```\r\npython -m pytest --doctest-modules pandas/core/frame.py::pandas.core.frame.DataFrame.info\r\n```\r\n\r\nWhere `pandas/core/frame.py` is the file where the docstring is defined, and\r\n`pandas.core.frame.DataFrame.info` is the object. A whole file can also be tested\r\nby removing the `::` and the object from the command above.\r\n\r\nIn general, the errors in the examples can be fixed with things like:\r\n\r\n- Fixing a typo (a missing comma, an mispelled variable name...)\r\n- Adding an object that hasn\'t been defined (like, if `df` is used, but\r\n  no sample dataset `df` has been first defined)\r\n- Fixing the expected output, when it\'s wrong\r\n- In exceptional cases, examples shouldn\'t run, since they can\'t work.\r\n  For example, a function that connects to a private webservice. In\r\n  such cases, we can add `# doctest: +SKIP` at the end of the lines\r\n  that should not run\r\n\r\nTo be able to properly fix an example for the first time, the next steps\r\nare needed:\r\n\r\n- Install a pandas development environment in your computer. There are\r\n  simplified instructions [in this page](https://python-sprints.github.io/pandas/guide/pandas_setup.html),\r\n  and more detailed information in [pandas official contributing page](https://pandas.pydata.org/docs/development/index.html).\r\n- Run the doctests for the object of interest (the one in this issue),\r\n  and make sure the examples are still broken in the `master` branch of\r\n  pandas\r\n- Fix the file locally, and run the doctests again, to make sure the\r\n  fix is working as expected\r\n- Optionally have a look and make sure that the code in the examples\r\n  follow PEP-8, and fix the style if it doesn\'t\r\n- Commit your changes, push your branch to a fork, and open a pull\r\n  request. Make sure you edit the line `Closes #XXXX` with the issue\r\n  number you are addressing, so the issue is automatically closed,\r\n  when the pull request is merged\r\n- Make sure the continuous integration of your pull request finishes\r\n  in green. If it doesn\'t, check if the problem is in your changes\r\n  (sometimes things break in master for technical problems, and in\r\n  that case you just need to wait for a core developer to fix the\r\n  problem)\r\n- Address any comment from the reviewers (just make changes locally,\r\n  commit, and push to your branch, no need to open new pull requests)',

There are\r\n  simplified instructions [in this page](https://python-sprints.github.io/pandas/guide/pandas_setup.html),\r\n  and more detailed information in [pandas official contributing page](https://pandas.pydata.org/docs/development/index.html).\r\n- Run the doctests for the object of interest (the one in this issue),\r\n  and make sure the examples are still broken in the `master` branch of\r\n  pandas\r\n- Fix the file locally, and run the doctests again, to make sure the\r\n  fix is working as expected\r\n- Optionally have a look and make sure that the code in the examples\r\n  follow PEP-8, and fix the style if it doesn\'t\r\n- Commit your changes, push your branch to a fork, and open a pull\r\n  request. Make sure you edit the line `Closes #XXXX` with the issue\r\n  number you are addressing, so the issue is automatically closed,\r\n  when the pull request is merged\r\n- Make sure the continuous integration of your pull request finishes\r\n  in green. If it doesn\'t, check if the problem is in your changes\r\n  (sometimes things break in master for technical problems, and in\r\n  that case you just need to wait for a core developer to fix the\r\n  problem)\r\n- Address any comment from the reviewers (just make changes locally,\r\n  commit, and push to your branch, no need to open new pull requests)',

And there are tools, like pytest,\r\nthat can run the examples, and make sure everything is correct.\r\n\r\nFor historical reasons, we have many examples where the code fails to run, or the\r\nactual output is different from the expected output. For example, check the next\r\nincorrect examples:\r\n\r\n```python\r\ndef add(num1, num2):\r\n    """\r\n    Computes the sum of the two numbers.\r\n\r\n    Examples\r\n    --------\r\n    >>> add(2, 2)\r\n    5\r\n\r\n    >>> add(2, 2\r\n    4\r\n\r\n    >>> add(2, number)\r\n    4\r\n\r\n    ...\r\n    """\r\n    return num1 + num2\r\n```\r\n\r\nAll them will fail for different reasons. To test the docstring of an object,\r\nthe next command can be run:\r\n\r\n```\r\npython -m pytest --doctest-modules pandas/core/frame.py::pandas.core.frame.DataFrame.info\r\n```\r\n\r\nWhere `pandas/core/frame.py` is the file where the docstring is defined, and\r\n`pandas.core.frame.DataFrame.info` is the object. A whole file can also be tested\r\nby removing the `::` and the object from the command above.\r\n\r\nIn general, the errors in the examples can be fixed with things like:\r\n\r\n- Fixing a typo (a missing comma, an mispelled variable name...)\r\n- Adding an object that hasn\'t been defined (like, if `df` is used, but\r\n  no sample dataset `df` has been first defined)\r\n- Fixing the expected output, when it\'s wrong\r\n- In exceptional cases, examples shouldn\'t run, since they can\'t work.\r\n  For example, a function that connects to a private webservice. I suggest simply returning the new table object, which is of type `sqlalchemy.Table`.\r\n\r\n#### API breaking implications\r\n\r\nNone, as `to_sql()` currently has no return value.\r\n\r\n#### Describe alternatives you've considered\r\n\r\n* You can query the table immediately using raw SQL as shown in the documentation for this function, but this is relatively low-level\r\n* You could obtain a `Table` object from the [`automap`](https://docs.sqlalchemy.org/en/14/orm/extensions/automap.html) extension. However this is redundant as Pandas at some point generated the table metadata so this would involve throwing it away and then trying to guess what it used to be from the state of the database.\r\n\r\n#### Additional context\r\n\r\nThis conflicts with #23998, which suggests that we return the `ResultProxy` instead. #data中的每个元素都是一个包含github问题页面上所有数据的字典

```python
issues=pd.DataFrame(data,columns=['number','title','labels','state'])
```

```python
#####6.4 与数据库交互 Interacting with Databases
#通常，企业中的数据不是存储在文本或Excel文件中的
#而是基于SQL的关系型数据库
#SQL Server，PostgreSQL,MySQL等


##数据库连接
##执行sql语句
##提交
##关闭连接

#使用sqlite3创建数据库的连接
import sqlite3
```


```python
#数据库连接
#sql命令
#在python中用三引号创建一个多行文本变量
#该变量为sql命令
#用于创建一个名叫test的表格
#里面有四列数据
query="""
CREATE TABLE test
(a VARCHAR(20),b VARCHAR(20),
c REAL,        d INTEGER
);"""
#其中a和b字段是字符串类型，最长20
#c是十进制8位存储
#d是整数类型
```


```python
#打开或创建数据库文件
#当我们指定的数据库文件不存在的时候
#连接对象会自动创建数据库文件
#如果数据库文件已经存在，直接打开该数据库文件
con =sqlite3.connect('mydata.sqlite')
```


```python
#其中.sqlite,表面该文件的类型是文件型数据库
##执行命令
con.execute(query)
```




    <sqlite3.Cursor at 0x2043df222d0>




```python
##提交命令
#对数据库产生修改的语句，要commit才会生效
#如果是查询，就只要execute提交语句
con.commit()
```


```python
##执行多条命令并提交
#将数据一行一行插进去
data=[('Atlanta','Georgia',1.25,6),
     ('Tallahassee','Florida',2.6,3),
     ('Sacramento','California',1.7,5)]
stmt="INSERT INTO test VALUES(?,?,?,?)"
con.executemany(stmt,data)
con.commit()
```


```python
##读出所有数据
#select * from test
#*是通配符，类似正则表达式，在test表格里读出所有数据
```


```python
cursor=con.execute('select * from test')
cursor
```




    <sqlite3.Cursor at 0x2043df31110>




```python
#返回的东西类似一个指针，指向数据表中的某一行，以此类推的话就一定是一个可迭代对象
#使用fetchall()函数读出
rows=cursor.fetchall()
rows
```




    [('Atlanta', 'Georgia', 1.25, 6),
     ('Tallahassee', 'Florida', 2.6, 3),
     ('Sacramento', 'California', 1.7, 5),
     ('Atlanta', 'Georgia', 1.25, 6),
     ('Tallahassee', 'Florida', 2.6, 3),
     ('Sacramento', 'California', 1.7, 5)]




```python
#这里读出类表格内容，但是没有读出列名
#列名在cursor的description属性中，所以，我们可以将它读出
for x in cursor.description:
    print(x[0])
    
```

    a
    b
    c
    d
    


```python
#将列名作为DataFrame的columns，row作为每行的值，创建dataframe
cursor.description
pd.DataFrame(rows,columns=[x[0] for x in cursor.description])
```

```python
con.close()
```

```python
#sqlalchemy 也是一个库
import sqlalchemy as sqla
db=sqla.create_engine('sqlite:///mydata.sqlite')
pd.read_sql('select * from test',db)
```

```python

```
